        var currentUrl=location.href;
        var vstart=currentUrl.indexOf(".cn/")+4;
        var vend=0;
        var vflag=false;
        if(currentUrl.indexOf("/?pvareaid=")>=0)
        {
            vend=currentUrl.indexOf("/?pvareaid=")-vstart;
            vflag=true;
        }
        var indexCityName="";
        if(!vflag)
        {
            indexCityName=currentUrl.substr(vstart).replace("/","");
        }
        else
        {
            indexCityName=currentUrl.substr(vstart,vend);
        }
        if (indexCityName == ''||indexCityName==undefined) {            
            indexCityName = Auto.findNameById(indexCityId, allAreaJson, defaultCityName);           
        }
        else {
            var foundCityId = Auto.findIdByName(indexCityName, allAreaJson);
            if (!foundCityId) {//没有对应的城市
                indexCityName = Auto.findNameById(indexCityId, allAreaJson, defaultCityName);  
            } 
            else {
                if (foundCityId != indexCityId&&indexCityId) {
                    indexCityId = foundCityId;
                    var options = {
                        expireHours: 36000 * 24,
                        domain: ".autohome.com.cn"
                    };
                    Auto.setCookie('cookieCityId', foundCityId, options);
                }
            }
